10.21 Self-service check-in at 5pm. The room I chose did not indicate whether it was facing the street. I was afraid of noise with my children, so I chose the innermost one because I took the subway. After walking a while, I felt a little sweaty, so I turned on the air conditioner. The effect was very average. I thought it was because it was turned on for a short time. I went out for dinner at about 8pm and returned. The air conditioner panel showed that the indoor temperature was 28 degrees. I adjusted it to the maximum wind speed of 20 degrees. It didn't help for one or two hours. I opened the window. It was very noisy facing the street. At about 9pm, the children were about to go to bed. They kept telling me that it was so hot. At this time, I suspected that the air conditioner host was not turned on. I called the front desk. The front desk said to adjust the temperature in the background. About five minutes later, a staff member knocked on the door and said that the host was not turned on, and only the fresh air was turned on. At this time, I was very speechless. The child couldn't sleep because it was very hot. He was sweating even wearing a very thin top. 
After 10 o'clock, the child still couldn't fall asleep. The twin beds I ordered only the inner bed could get a little wind, and the outer bed had no wind at all. To open the window, you must open the curtains I opened the curtains and the lights were on outside. It was very noisy and I couldn't fall asleep. I kept fanning the kids and opening the windows. I repeated this for two hours. The kids finally fell asleep and I was exhausted.
I really want to ask the hotel management. It's a west-facing hotel with a temperature of 30 degrees during the day and 28 degrees indoors. Isn't it worth turning on an air conditioner? ! The staff said that there were guests who were afraid of the cold. Didn't they know not to turn on the air conditioner? What a **
I really avoid this hotel. I don't want to give it a single star. I will never go there again. I also hope that everyone will ask whether the air conditioner is turned on before staying there. With a room rate of nearly 400, is it really necessary to do this? ! ! ! ?
